        (function() {
      let adFlag = true
      //Check optimera smart refresh enabled or not
      if(trb.data.ads.optimera && (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) && (true)) {
        let oInsights = window.oVa.insights ? window.oVa.insights : {}
        let oRemoveAds = oInsights.ilv ? oInsights.ilv : ''
        if(oRemoveAds.indexOf('trb_ad_1280x220/970x250/970x90/728x90/320x100/320x50_1_/') != -1 && true) {
          let label = document.getElementById('label_hp_122')
          label && label.classList.add('hddn')
          adFlag = false
        }
      }
      if(adFlag) {
        
          //FetchBids for all ads
          if (((!DeviceDetection.isDesktopSize() && false) || (DeviceDetection.isDesktopSize() && true)) && (true && window.apstag) && ((true && window.headertag) || (true && window.PWT))) {
            let params = {
              id: 'hp_122',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.sunsentinel/hp',
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true
            }
            if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor = trb.data.page.ads.vendor || {}
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams = trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams || {}
            }
            const dimensions = !' [[[1280, 220], [970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [320, 100], [320, 50]]] '.length ? null : JSON.parse(' [[[1280, 220], [970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [320, 100], [320, 50]]] '),
              sizemapDimensions = !'[[1280, 0], [800, 0], [0, 0]]'.length ? null : JSON.parse('[[1280, 0], [800, 0], [0, 0]]')
            if (sizemapDimensions) {
              const mapping = DFPHelpers.prepareSizeMaps(dimensions, sizemapDimensions).mapping
              const parsedMapping = DFPHelpers.parseSizeMappings(mapping)
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_122'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : parsedMapping}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(parsedMapping, params)
            } else {
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_122'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : dimensions}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(dimensions, params)
            }
          }

          
            if (trb.data.ads.optimera) {
              if (!window.oPageUnload) {
                oAv.push("trb_ad_1280x220/970x250/970x90/728x90/320x100/320x50_1_/");
                oVa["trb_ad_1280x220/970x250/970x90/728x90/320x100/320x50_1_/"] = ["NULL"];
              } else {
                oPageUnload('trb_ad_1280x220/970x250/970x90/728x90/320x100/320x50_1_/', true);
              }
            }
          
          function loadAd() {
            dfpService.appendAd({
              id: 'hp_122',
              optimeraId: 'trb_ad_1280x220/970x250/970x90/728x90/320x100/320x50_1_/',
              adType: 'leaderboard',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.sunsentinel/hp',
              displayMobile: false,
              displayDesktop: true,
              isOOP: false,
              is5x1: false,
              dimensionsString: ' [[[1280, 220], [970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [320, 100], [320, 50]]] ',

              refreshOnPhotoChange: false,
              adRefreshInterval: 0,
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true,
              isMobileSticky: false,
              loadImmediately: true
            }, false, true)
          }
          loadAd();
        
      }
    })()
